<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To create a controlled Tooltip component, manage the state of whether the tooltip is open using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">open</code> prop:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the tooltip is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useTooltip</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="arrow" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Arrow</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To display an arrow pointing to the trigger from the tooltip, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Tooltip.Arrow</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Tooltip.ArrowTip</code> components:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="delay" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#delay"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Delay</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To configure the open and close delay for the Tooltip, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeDelay</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">openDelay</code> props:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="positioning" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#positioning"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Positioning</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To customize the position of the Tooltip relative to the trigger, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">positioning</code> prop:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the tooltip&#x27;s state and methods with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Tooltip.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useTooltipContext</code> hook:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="within-fixed-containers" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#within-fixed-containers"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Within Fixed Containers</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When rendering a tooltip inside a fixed-position container, set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">positioning.strategy</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&quot;fixed&quot;</code> to ensure proper
positioning.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>

-->data-scope<!-- -->]</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">tooltip</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">[<!-- -->data-part<!-- -->]</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">trigger</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">[<!-- -->data-expanded<!-- -->]</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Present when expanded</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">[<!-- -->data-state<!-- -->]</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">API</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Property</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">open</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether the tooltip is open.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">setOpen</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to open the tooltip.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">reposition</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(options?: Partial&lt;PositioningOptions&gt;) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to reposition the popover</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/tooltip/" class="link">Tooltip WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>

controlled Tooltip component, manage the state of whether the tooltip is open using the `open` prop:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/react/tooltip'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e setOpen(!open)} className={button.Root}\u003e\n        Toggle\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Root open={open} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cTooltip.Content className={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/solid/tooltip'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = createSignal(false)\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e setOpen(!open())}\u003e\n        Toggle\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Root open={open()} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/vue/tooltip'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nconst open = ref(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cbutton @click=\"open = !open\"\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Root v-model:open=\"open\"\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tooltip'\n  import styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\n  let open = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cbutton onclick={() =\u003e (open = !open)}\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n\n\u003cTooltip.Root bind:open\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the tooltip is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useTooltip` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tooltip, useTooltip } from '@ark-ui/react/tooltip'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const tooltip = useTooltip()\n\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eOpen: {String(tooltip.open)}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.RootProvider value={tooltip}\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cTooltip.Content className={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tooltip, useTooltip } from '@ark-ui/solid/tooltip'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const tooltip = useTooltip()\n\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003cbutton onClick={() =\u003e tooltip().setOpen(true)}\u003eOpen\u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cTooltip.RootProvider value={tooltip}\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tooltip, useTooltip } from '@ark-ui/vue/tooltip'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nconst tooltip = useTooltip()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cbutton @click=\"tooltip.setOpen(true)\"\u003eOpen\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cTooltip.RootProvider :value=\"tooltip\"\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Tooltip, useTooltip } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tooltip'\n  import styles from tooltip().setOpen(true)}\u003eOpen\u003c/button\u003e\n\n\u003cTooltip.RootProvider value={tooltip}\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Tooltip.RootProvider\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Arrow\n\nTo display an arrow pointing to the trigger from the tooltip, use the `Tooltip.Arrow` and `Tooltip.ArrowTip`  }\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tooltip'\n  import styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cTooltip.Root positioning={{ placement: 'left-start', offset: { mainAxis: 12, crossAxis: 12 } }}\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess the tooltip's state and methods with `Tooltip.Context` or the `useTooltipContext` hook:\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/react/tooltip'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTooltip.Root\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Context\u003e\n          {(tooltip) =\u003e (\n            \u003cTooltip.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              This tooltip is open: {tooltip.open.toString()}\n            \u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Tooltip.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/solid/tooltip'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTooltip.Root\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Context\u003e\n          {(context) =\u003e (\n            \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eThis tooltip is open: {context().open.toString()}\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Tooltip.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/vue/tooltip'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Root\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Context v-slot=\"tooltip\"\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003eThis tooltip is open: {{ tooltip.open.toString() }}\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Tooltip.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tooltip'\n  import styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cTooltip.Root\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Context\u003e\n        {#snippet render(context)}\n          \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n            This tooltip is open: {context().open.toString()}\n          \u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n        {/snippet}\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Within Fixed Containers\n\nWhen rendering a tooltip inside a fixed-position container, set `positioning.strategy` to `\"fixed\"` to ensure proper\npositioning.\n\n**Example: within-fixed**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/react/tooltip'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const WithinFixed = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cdiv style={{ position: 'fixed', top: '40px', left: '40px', padding: '40px', background: 'red' }}\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Root positioning={{ strategy: 'fixed' }}\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Content className={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/solid/tooltip'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\nexport const WithinFixed = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cdiv style={{ position: 'fixed', top: '40px', left: '40px', padding: '40px', background: 'red' }}\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Root positioning={{ strategy: 'fixed' }}\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/vue/tooltip'\nimport styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"position: fixed; top: 40px; left: 40px; padding: 40px; background: red\"\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Root :positioning=\"{ strategy: 'fixed' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n          \u003cTooltip.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n    \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { Tooltip } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tooltip'\n  import styles from 'styles/tooltip.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv style=\"position: fixed; top: 40px; left: 40px; padding: 40px; background: red\"\u003e\n  \u003cTooltip.Root positioning={{ strategy: 'fixed' }}\u003e\n    \u003cTooltip.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eHover Me\u003c/Tooltip.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cTooltip.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003cTooltip.Content class={styles.Content}\u003eI am a tooltip!\u003c/Tooltip.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Tooltip.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Tooltip.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `aria-label` | `string` | No | Custom label for the tooltip. |\n| `closeDelay` | `number` | No | The close delay of the tooltip. |\n| `closeOnClick` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip should close on click |\n| `closeOnEscape` | `boolean` | No | Whether to close the tooltip when the Escape key is pressed. |\n| `closeOnPointerDown` | `boolean` | No | Whether to close the tooltip on pointerdown. |\n| `closeOnScroll` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip should close on scroll |\n| `defaultOpen` | `boolean` | No | The initial open state of the tooltip when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the open state of the tooltip. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip is disabled |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ trigger: string; content: string; arrow: string; positioner: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the tooltip. Useful for composition. |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `interactive` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip's content is interactive.\nIn this mode, the tooltip will remain open when user hovers over the content. |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `onOpenChange` | `(details: OpenChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the tooltip is opened. |\n| `open` | `boolean` | No | The controlled open state of the tooltip |\n| `openDelay` | `number` | No | The open delay of the tooltip. |\n| `positioning` | `PositioningOptions` | No | The user provided options used to position the popover content |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled by the user) |\n| `skipAnimationOnMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the initial presence animation. |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**Arrow Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Arrow CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--arrow-size` | The size of the arrow |\n| `--arrow-size-half` | Half the size of the arrow |\n| `--arrow-background` | Use this variable to style the arrow background |\n| `--arrow-offset` | The offset position of the arrow |\n\n\n**ArrowTip Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | tooltip |\n| `[data-part]` | content |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n| `[data-instant]` |  |\n| `[data-placement]` | The placement of the content |\n\n\n**Positioner Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Positioner CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--reference-width` | The width of the reference element |\n| `--reference-height` | The height of the root |\n| `--available-width` | The available width in viewport |\n| `--available-height` | The available height in viewport |\n| `--x` | The x position for transform |\n| `--y` | The y position for transform |\n| `--z-index` | The z-index value |\n| `--transform-origin` | The transform origin for animations |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UseTooltipReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled by the user) |\n| `skipAnimationOnMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the initial presence animation. |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**Trigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Trigger Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | tooltip |\n| `[data-part]` | trigger |\n| `[data-expanded]` | Present when expanded |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n\n\n#### Solid\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `aria-label` | `string` | No | Custom label for the tooltip. |\n| `closeDelay` | `number` | No | The close delay of the tooltip. |\n| `closeOnClick` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip should close on click |\n| `closeOnEscape` | `boolean` | No | Whether to close the tooltip when the Escape key is pressed. |\n| `closeOnPointerDown` | `boolean` | No | Whether to close the tooltip on pointerdown. |\n| `closeOnScroll` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip should close on scroll |\n| `defaultOpen` | `boolean` | No | The initial open state of the tooltip when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the open state of the tooltip. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip is disabled |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ trigger: string; content: string; arrow: string; positioner: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the tooltip. Useful for composition. |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `interactive` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip's content is interactive.\nIn this mode, the tooltip will remain open when user hovers over the content. |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `onOpenChange` | `(details: OpenChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the tooltip is opened. |\n| `open` | `boolean` | No | The controlled open state of the tooltip |\n| `openDelay` | `number` | No | The open delay of the tooltip. |\n| `positioning` | `PositioningOptions` | No | The user provided options used to position the popover content |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled by the user) |\n| `skipAnimationOnMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the initial presence animation. |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**Arrow Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Arrow CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--arrow-size` | The size of the arrow |\n| `--arrow-size-half` | Half the size of the arrow |\n| `--arrow-background` | Use this variable to style the arrow background |\n| `--arrow-offset` | The offset position of the arrow |\n\n\n**ArrowTip Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | tooltip |\n| `[data-part]` | content |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n| `[data-instant]` |  |\n| `[data-placement]` | The placement of the content |\n\n\n**Positioner Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Positioner CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--reference-width` | The width of the reference element |\n| `--reference-height` | The height of the root |\n| `--available-width` | The available width in viewport |\n| `--available-height` | The available height in viewport |\n| `--x` | The x position for transform |\n| `--y` | The y position for transform |\n| `--z-index` | The z-index value |\n| `--transform-origin` | The transform origin for animations |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UseTooltipReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'button'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child tooltip when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the open state of the tooltip. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip is disabled |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique Useful for composition. |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `interactive` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tooltip's content is interactive.\nIn this mode, the tooltip will remain open when user hovers over the content. |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `onOpenChange` | `(details: OpenChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the tooltip is opened. |\n| `open` | `boolean` | No | The controlled open state of the tooltip |\n| `openDelay` | `number` | No | The open delay of the tooltip. |\n| `positioning` | `PositioningOptions` | No | The user provided options used to position the popover content |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled by the user) |\n| `skipAnimationOnMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the initial presence animation. |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**Arrow Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description
